import os
import sys

if sys.version_info[:2] >= (3, 0):

    def exec_file_wrapper(fpath, g_vars, l_vars):
        with open(fpath) as f:
            code = compile(f.read(), os.path.basename(fpath), "exec")
            exec(code, g_vars, l_vars)
